+def _kernel(
+    A_ptr, W_gate_ptr, W_up_ptr, Out_ptr,
+    block_to_expert_ptr, block_to_m_abs_ptr,
+    H, N,
+    num_m_blocks, num_n_blocks, num_tiles,
+    stride_am, stride_ak,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_om, stride_on,
+    NUM_SMS: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    GROUP_M: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    for tile_id in range(pid, num_tiles, NUM_SMS):
+        num_pid_in_group = GROUP_M * num_n_blocks
+        group_id = tile_id // num_pid_in_group
+        first_pid_m = group_id * GROUP_M
+        group_size_m = min(num_m_blocks - first_pid_m, GROUP_M)
+        pid_m = first_pid_m + ((tile_id % num_pid_in_group) % group_size_m)
+        pid_n = (tile_id % num_pid_in_group) // group_size_m
+
+        e = tl.load(block_to_expert_ptr + pid_m)
+        m_abs = tl.load(block_to_m_abs_ptr + pid_m)
+        offs_m = m_abs + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+        offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+        a_ptrs = A_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_am + offs_k[None, :] * stride_ak
+        w_gate_ptrs = W_gate_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn
+        w_up_ptrs = W_up_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for k in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            a = tl.load(a_ptrs)
+            w_g = tl.load(w_gate_ptrs)
+            w_u = tl.load(w_up_ptrs)
+            acc_g = tl.dot(a, w_g, acc=acc_g)
+            acc_u = tl.dot(a, w_u, acc=acc_u)
+            a_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_ak
+            w_gate_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+            w_up_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
+        out = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+        o_ptrs = Out_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_om + offs_n[None, :] * stride_on
+        tl.store(o_ptrs, out)
+
+
+def _build_block_table(expert_offsets, E, BLOCK_M):
+    offsets_cpu = expert_offsets.cpu().to(torch.int64)
+    block_to_expert, block_to_m_abs = [], []
+    for e in range(E):
+        start = int(offsets_cpu[e].item())
+        end = int(offsets_cpu[e + 1].item())
+        n_e = end - start
+        if n_e == 0: continue
+        n_blocks = (n_e + BLOCK_M - 1) // BLOCK_M
+        for b in range(n_blocks):
+            block_to_expert.append(e)
+            block_to_m_abs.append(start + b * BLOCK_M)
+    return (
+        torch.tensor(block_to_expert, dtype=torch.int32, device=expert_offsets.device),
+        torch.tensor(block_to_m_abs, dtype=torch.int32, device=expert_offsets.device),
+    )
+
+
+def time_kernel_cuda(fn, n_warmup=5, n_iter=20):
+    for _ in range(n_warmup):
+        fn()
+    torch.cuda.synchronize()
+    s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
+    e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
+    s.record()
+    for _ in range(n_iter):
+        fn()
+    e.record()
+    torch.cuda.synchronize()
+    return s.elapsed_time(e) / n_iter
+
+
+shapes = [
+    {'T_total': 32768, 'H': 4096, 'I': 1536, 'E': 128, 'K': 8},
+    {'T_total': 4096, 'H': 2048, 'I': 1024, 'E': 64, 'K': 4},
+    {'T_total': 16384, 'H': 2048, 'I': 4096, 'E': 64, 'K': 8},
+]
+
+import reference as ref
+
+configs = [
+    (64, 64, 64, 4, 4, 4),
+    (64, 64, 64, 4, 5, 4),
+    (64, 64, 64, 4, 6, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 4, 5, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 4, 6, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 4, 7, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 4, 8, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 8, 4, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 8, 5, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 8, 6, 4),
+    (64, 256, 32, 8, 3, 4),
+    (64, 256, 32, 8, 4, 4),
+    (64, 256, 32, 8, 5, 4),
+    (128, 32, 64, 4, 4, 4),
+    (128, 32, 64, 4, 5, 4),
+    (128, 32, 64, 4, 6, 4),
+    (128, 32, 64, 8, 4, 4),
+    (128, 128, 32, 4, 4, 4),
+    (128, 128, 32, 4, 5, 4),
+    (128, 128, 32, 8, 4, 4),
+    # 16xN configs
+    (16, 64, 64, 4, 8, 4),
+    (16, 64, 64, 4, 10, 4),
+    (16, 64, 64, 4, 12, 4),
+    (16, 128, 64, 4, 5, 4),
+    (16, 128, 64, 4, 6, 4),
+    (32, 64, 64, 4, 6, 4),
+    (32, 64, 64, 4, 8, 4),
+]
+
+for shape in shapes:
+    print(f'\n=== Shape: {shape} ===')
+    ref.T_total = shape['T_total']; ref.H = shape['H']; ref.I = shape['I']; ref.E = shape['E']; ref.K = shape['K']
+
+    init_args = ref.get_init_inputs()
+    ref_model = ref.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
+    W_gate = ref_model.W_gate
+    W_up = ref_model.W_up
+    hidden = torch.randn(shape['T_total']*shape['K'], shape['H'], dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda') * 0.1
+    T_perm = shape['T_total'] * shape['K']
+    base = T_perm // shape['E']
+    rem = T_perm - base * shape['E']
+    counts = torch.full((shape['E'],), base, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
+    counts[:rem] += 1
+    offsets = torch.zeros(shape['E']+1, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
+    offsets[1:] = torch.cumsum(counts, dim=0)
+
+    for BM, BN, BK, nw, ns, gm in configs:
+        try:
+            bte, btma = _build_block_table(offsets, shape['E'], BM)
+            nmb = bte.shape[0]
+            nnb = (shape['I'] + BN - 1) // BN
+            nt = nmb * nnb
+            out = torch.empty(T_perm, shape['I'], dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+
+            def fn(h=hidden, o=offsets, wg=W_gate, wu=W_up, BM=BM, BN=BN, BK=BK, nw=nw, ns=ns, gm=gm, bte=bte, btma=btma, nmb=nmb, nnb=nnb, nt=nt, out=out):
+                _kernel[(188,)](
+                    h, wg, wu, out,
+                    bte, btma,
+                    shape['H'], shape['I'],
+                    nmb, nnb, nt,
+                    h.stride(0), h.stride(1),
+                    wg.stride(0), wg.stride(1), wg.stride(2),
+

+"""Test a CUDA C++ kernel for comparison with Triton."""
+import os
+os.environ['TORCH_CUDA_ARCH_LIST'] = '12.0'
+
+import torch
+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+# CUDA kernel source for grouped GEMM with SwiGLU
+# Each block handles one (m, n) tile, computing gemm + silu * up
+cuda_source = r"""
+#include <cuda_runtime.h>
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+#include <torch/extension.h>
+
+// A simple grouped GEMM kernel. Not the most optimized, but a starting point.
+// Each block handles one (m_block, n_block) tile.
+// A, W_gate, W_up are bf16, accumulator is fp32.
+
+__global__ void grouped_gemm_swiglu_kernel(
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ A,         // (T_perm, H)
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ W_gate,    // (E, H, I)
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ W_up,      // (E, H, I)
+    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ Out,             // (T_perm, I)
+    const int* __restrict__ block_to_expert,     // (num_m_blocks,)
+    const int* __restrict__ block_to_m_abs,      // (num_m_blocks,)
+    int num_m_blocks, int num_n_blocks,
+    int H, int I
+) {
+    int pid_m = blockIdx.x;
+    int pid_n = blockIdx.y;
+    if (pid_m >= num_m_blocks || pid_n >= num_n_blocks) return;
+
+    int e = block_to_expert[pid_m];
+    int m_abs = block_to_m_abs[pid_m];
+
+    const int BLOCK_M = 64;
+    const int BLOCK_N = 64;
+    const int BLOCK_K = 32;
+
+    int tid = threadIdx.x;
+    int warp_id = tid / 32;
+    int lane = tid % 32;
+
+    // Shared memory tiles
+    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 a_smem[BLOCK_M][BLOCK_K];
+    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 wg_smem[BLOCK_K][BLOCK_N];
+    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 wu_smem[BLOCK_K][BLOCK_N];
+
+    // Each thread accumulates a portion of the (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N) output
+    // For simplicity, use 8x8 tiles per warp = 64x64 total with 8 warps
+    // We use 4 warps here for now.
+    const int WARPS_M = 2;  // 2 warps in M direction
+    const int WARPS_N = 2;  // 2 warps in N direction
+    const int WARP_M = 16;
+    const int WARP_N = 32;
+
+    int warp_m = warp_id / WARPS_N;
+    int warp_n = warp_id % WARPS_N;
+
+    float acc_g[WARP_M / 8][WARP_N / 8][4] = {0};  // 2x4x4 = 32 fp32
+    float acc_u[WARP_M / 8][WARP_N / 8][4] = {0};
+
+    // K loop
+    for (int k = 0; k < H; k += BLOCK_K) {
+        // Cooperative load of A tile (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_K)
+        // Each thread loads (BLOCK_M * BLOCK_K) / (4 * 32) = 64 / 32 = 2 elements
+        for (int i = 0; i < (BLOCK_M * BLOCK_K) / (4 * 32); i++) {
+            int idx = i * 128 + tid;
+            int row = idx / BLOCK_K;
+            int col = idx % BLOCK_K;
+            int g_row = m_abs + row;
+            int g_col = k + col;
+            a_smem[row][col] = A[g_row * H + g_col];
+        }
+        // Cooperative load of W_gate tile (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N)
+        for (int i = 0; i < (BLOCK_K * BLOCK_N) / (4 * 32); i++) {
+            int idx = i * 128 + tid;
+            int row = idx / BLOCK_N;
+            int col = idx % BLOCK_N;
+            int g_row = k + row;
+            int g_col = pid_n * BLOCK_N + col;
+            wg_smem[row][col] = W_gate[e * H * I + g_row * I + g_col];
+            wu_smem[row][col] = W_up[e * H * I + g_row * I + g_col];
+        }
+        __syncthreads();
+
+        // MMA: (WARP_M, WARP_N) per warp
+        // For simplicity, just do scalar multiplies for now (very slow)
+        // TODO: use mma.sync
+
+        __syncthreads();
+    }
+
+    // Write output (WARP_M, WARP_N) per warp
+    // For now skip - the kernel is incomplete
+}
+
+void grouped_gemm_swiglu(
+    torch::Tensor A, torch::Tensor W_gate, torch::Tensor W_up,
+    torch::Tensor Out, torch::Tensor block_to_expert, torch::Tensor block_to_m_abs,
+    int num_m_blocks, int num_n_blocks
+) {
+    int H = A.size(1);
+    int I = W_gate.size(2);
+    dim3 grid(num_m_blocks, num_n_blocks);
+    dim3 block(128);
+    grouped_gemm_swiglu_kernel<<<grid, block>>>(
+        (__nv_bf16*)A.data_ptr(), (__nv_bf16*)W_gate.data_ptr(),
+        (__nv_bf16*)W_up.data_ptr(), (__nv_bf16*)Out.data_ptr(),
+        block_to_expert.data_ptr<int>(), block_to_m_abs.data_ptr<int>(),
+        num_m_blocks, num_n_blocks, H, I
+    );
+}
+"""
+
+cpp_source = r"""
+void grouped_gemm_swiglu(
+    torch::Tensor A, torch::Tensor W_gate, torch::Tensor W_up,
+    torch::Tensor Out, torch::Tensor block_to_expert, torch::Tensor block_to_m_abs,
+    int num_m_blocks, int num_n_blocks
+);
+"""
+
+# Note: this CUDA kernel is incomplete - just demonstrates the structure
+# A proper implementation would use mma.sync instructions.
+# For the actual submission, we'll use the Triton kernel.
+print("CUDA kernel template created. Skipping compilation test.")

reasoning (1847 chars)
Writing a complete CUDA kernel with proper mma.sync instructions is a significant effort. Let me focus on what I can do quickly. Let me look at the solution once more and make sure it's good. We're at 22.4% peak. Let me also try one more thing: use the W concat with proper handling. Actually, the merged dot has a known issue with layout. Let me look at how to fix it properly. The dot output of (BM, K) @ (K, 2*BN) has shape (BM, 2*BN). The "natural" interpretation is row-major. But the MMA produces a different layout. For m16n8k16 MMA: the output of one MMA is 16*8 = 128 fp32 values. These are distributed across 32 threads (1 warp), 4 fp32 per thread. For a (BM, 2*BN) = (128, 128) dot, we have 8 (M) * 16 (N) = 128 MMAs. With 4 warps, each warp does 32 MMAs. The 128 MMAs are arranged as 8 M tiles and 16 N tiles, with each M tile being 16 rows and each N tile being 8 cols. The output layout: thread (warp, lane) holds acc[warp_m][warp_n] where warp_m is in [0, 8) and warp_n is in [0, 16). For 4 warps, the 4 warps handle different (warp_m, warp_n) ranges. When we do `tl.reshape` on this layout, Triton may need to do a register shuffle to convert to row-major. Actually, in Triton, the dot output is in "tensor" form, which Triton abstracts from the physical layout. The reshape should work correctly IF the dot's output is logically a (BM, 2*BN) tensor. But the issue is that the split requires the output to be in a specific layout where the last dim can be split. Let me try one more approach: do TWO dots, but with the B tile loaded as a single (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) tile, and split it via tl.split before the dot. The B tile is loaded via tl.load, which gives a (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) tensor in row-major layout. Reshape to (BLOCK_K, 2, BLOCK_N) and split into two (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N) tensors should work. Let me try this.

+"""Test kernel with merged B load + split before dot."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kernel_split_b(
+    A_ptr, W_gate_ptr, W_up_ptr, Out_ptr,
+    block_to_expert_ptr, block_to_m_abs_ptr,
+    H, N,
+    num_m_blocks, num_n_blocks, num_tiles,
+    stride_am, stride_ak,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_om, stride_on,
+    NUM_SMS: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    GROUP_M: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Load a (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) W tile per expert (W_gate followed by W_up),
+    then split into two (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N) tiles for the two dots.
+    """
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    for tile_id in range(pid, num_tiles, NUM_SMS):
+        num_pid_in_group = GROUP_M * num_n_blocks
+        group_id = tile_id // num_pid_in_group
+        first_pid_m = group_id * GROUP_M
+        group_size_m = min(num_m_blocks - first_pid_m, GROUP_M)
+        pid_m = first_pid_m + ((tile_id % num_pid_in_group) % group_size_m)
+        pid_n = (tile_id % num_pid_in_group) // group_size_m
+
+        e = tl.load(block_to_expert_ptr + pid_m)
+        m_abs = tl.load(block_to_m_abs_ptr + pid_m)
+
+        offs_m = m_abs + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+        offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+
+        a_ptrs = A_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_am + offs_k[None, :] * stride_ak
+        # Single (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) load. The first BLOCK_N cols are W_gate,
+        # the last BLOCK_N cols are W_up. They must be in the same memory.
+        # We achieve this by passing the concat'd W.
+        w_combined_ptrs = (
+            W_gate_ptr + e * stride_we
+            + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk
+            + tl.arange(0, 2 * BLOCK_N)[None, :] * stride_wn
+        )
+
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+        for k in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            a = tl.load(a_ptrs)
+            w = tl.load(w_combined_ptrs)  # (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N)
+            # Split: (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) -> (BLOCK_K, 2, BLOCK_N) -> transpose -> (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N, 2) -> split
+            w_r = tl.reshape(w, (BLOCK_K, 2, BLOCK_N))
+            w_t = tl.trans(w_r, (0, 2, 1))  # (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N, 2)
+            w_g, w_u = tl.split(w_t)  # (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N), (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N)
+            acc_g = tl.dot(a, w_g, acc=acc_g)
+            acc_u = tl.dot(a, w_u, acc=acc_u)
+            a_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_ak
+            w_combined_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+
+        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
+        out = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+        o_ptrs = Out_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_om + offs_n[None, :] * stride_on
+        tl.store(o_ptrs, out)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kernel_separate(
+    A_ptr, W_gate_ptr, W_up_ptr, Out_ptr,
+    block_to_expert_ptr, block_to_m_abs_ptr,
+    H, N,
+    num_m_blocks, num_n_blocks, num_tiles,
+    stride_am, stride_ak,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_om, stride_on,
+    NUM_SMS: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    GROUP_M: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    for tile_id in range(pid, num_tiles, NUM_SMS):
+        num_pid_in_group = GROUP_M * num_n_blocks
+        group_id = tile_id // num_pid_in_group
+        first_pid_m = group_id * GROUP_M
+        group_size_m = min(num_m_blocks - first_pid_m, GROUP_M)
+        pid_m = first_pid_m + ((tile_id % num_pid_in_group) % group_size_m)
+        pid_n = (tile_id % num_pid_in_group) // group_size_m
+
+        e = tl.load(block_to_expert_ptr + pid_m)
+        m_abs = tl.load(block_to_m_abs_ptr + pid_m)
+        offs_m = m_abs + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+        offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+        a_ptrs = A_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_am + offs_k[None, :] * stride_ak
+        w_gate_ptrs = W_gate_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn
+        w_up_ptrs = W_up_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for k in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            a = tl.load(a_ptrs)
+            w_g = tl.load(w_gate_ptrs)
+            w_u = tl.load(w_up_ptrs)
+            acc_g = tl.dot(a, w_g, acc=acc_g)
+            acc_u = tl.dot(a, w_u, acc=acc_u)
+            a_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_ak
+            w_gate_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+            w_up_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
+        out = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+        o_ptrs = Out_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_om + offs_n[None, :] * stride_on
+        tl.store(o_ptrs, out)
+
+
+def _build_block_table(expert_offsets, E, BLOCK_M):
+    offsets_cpu = expert_offsets.cpu().to(torch.int64)
+    block_to_expert, block_to_m_abs = [], []
+    for e in range(E):
+        start = int(offsets_cpu[e].item())
+        end = int(offsets_cpu[e + 1].item())
+        n_e = end - start
+        if n_e == 0: continue
+        n_blocks = (n_e + BLOCK_M - 1) // BLOCK_M
+        for b in range(n_blocks):
+            block_to_expert.append(e)
+            block_to_m_abs.append(start + b * BLOCK_M)
+    return (
+        torch.tensor(block_to_expert, dtype=torch.int32, device=expert_offsets.device),
+        torch.tensor(block_to_m_abs, dtype=torch.int32, device=expert_offsets.device),
+    )
+
+
+def time_kernel_cuda(fn, n_warmup=5, n_iter=20):
+    for _ in range(n_warmup):
+        fn()
+    torch.cuda.synchronize()
+    s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
+    e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
+    s.record()

reasoning (2115 chars)
The split_b is both slower AND wrong. The diff is 0.21 for shape 0. So splitting the B tile via reshape+transpose+split is incorrect. The issue: when we load (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) and reshape to (BLOCK_K, 2, BLOCK_N), then transpose to (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N, 2), then split, the resulting tensors are INTERLEAVED, not contiguous halves. The original (BLOCK_K, 2*BLOCK_N) tile has: - row 0: [w_g[0,0], w_g[0,1], ..., w_g[0,BN-1], w_u[0,0], w_u[0,1], ..., w_u[0,BN-1]] After reshape to (BLOCK_K, 2, BLOCK_N): - (k, 0, l) = original[k, l] for l in [0, BN) = w_g[k, l] - (k, 1, l) = original[k, l + BN] for l in [0, BN) = w_u[k, l] After transpose (0, 2, 1) to (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N, 2): - (k, l, 0) = (k, 0, l) = w_g[k, l] - (k, l, 1) = (k, 1, l) = w_u[k, l] After split (last dim of size 2): - First tensor: w_g (k, l) = original (k, l) for l in [0, BN) - Second tensor: w_u (k, l) = original (k, l + BN) for l in [0, BN) So the split should give w_g as the first BN cols and w_u as the last BN cols. That's what we want! But the result is wrong. Why? Oh, I think the issue is that the dot output layout is different from what tl.dot expects as input. When we do `tl.dot(a, w_g)` where w_g came from a tl.split of a loaded tensor, the layout might not match. Hmm, let me check more carefully. The B tensor from a tl.load is in row-major layout. The reshape + transpose + split might preserve this. Wait, the split requires last dim of size 2. After reshape (BLOCK_K, 2, BLOCK_N) -> transpose -> (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N, 2). The last dim is 2. Split gives (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N) and (BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N). The resulting tensors are in some layout. When passed to tl.dot, the compiler may need to do a layout conversion. If the layout conversion is incorrect, the result would be wrong. Let me try a simpler approach: just use two separate loads (which is the current approach and works correctly). The "split the B tile" approach has correctness issues. OK the merged approach with split B doesn't work. Let me stop trying to merge and focus on making the current approach faster. +"""Final sweep over configs with current kernel structure."""
+import torch
+import time
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kernel(
+    A_ptr, W_gate_ptr, W_up_ptr, Out_ptr,
+    block_to_expert_ptr, block_to_m_abs_ptr,
+    H, N,
+    num_m_blocks, num_n_blocks, num_tiles,
+    stride_am, stride_ak,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_om, stride_on,
+    NUM_SMS: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    GROUP_M: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    for tile_id in range(pid, num_tiles, NUM_SMS):
+        num_pid_in_group = GROUP_M * num_n_blocks
+        group_id = tile_id // num_pid_in_group
+        first_pid_m = group_id * GROUP_M
+        group_size_m = min(num_m_blocks - first_pid_m, GROUP_M)
+        pid_m = first_pid_m + ((tile_id % num_pid_in_group) % group_size_m)
+        pid_n = (tile_id % num_pid_in_group) // group_size_m
+
+        e = tl.load(block_to_expert_ptr + pid_m)
+        m_abs = tl.load(block_to_m_abs_ptr + pid_m)
+        offs_m = m_abs + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+        offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+        a_ptrs = A_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_am + offs_k[None, :] * stride_ak
+        w_gate_ptrs = W_gate_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn
+        w_up_ptrs = W_up_ptr + e * stride_we + offs_k[:, None] * stride_wk + offs_n[None, :] * stride_wn
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for k in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            a = tl.load(a_ptrs)
+            w_g = tl.load(w_gate_ptrs)
+            w_u = tl.load(w_up_ptrs)
+            acc_g = tl.dot(a, w_g, acc=acc_g)
+            acc_u = tl.dot(a, w_u, acc=acc_u)
+            a_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_ak
+            w_gate_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+            w_up_ptrs += BLOCK_K * stride_wk
+        silu_g = acc_g * tl.sigmoid(acc_g)
+        out = (silu_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+        o_ptrs = Out_ptr + offs_m[:, None] * stride_om + offs_n[None, :] * stride_on
+        tl.store(o_ptrs, out)
+
+
+def _build_block_table(expert_offsets, E, BLOCK_M):
+    offsets_cpu = expert_offsets.cpu().to(torch.int64)
+    block_to_expert, block_to_m_abs = [], []
+    for e in range(E):
+        start = int(offsets_cpu[e].item())
+        end = int(offsets_cpu[e + 1].item())
+        n_e = end - start
+        if n_e == 0: continue
+        n_blocks = (n_e + BLOCK_M - 1) // BLOCK_M
+        for b in range(n_blocks):
+            block_to_expert.append(e)
+            block_to_m_abs.append(start + b * BLOCK_M)
+    return (
+        torch.tensor(block_to_expert, dtype=torch.int32, device=expert_offsets.device),
+        torch.tensor(block_to_m_abs, dtype=torch.int32, device=expert_offsets.device),
+    )
+
+
+def time_kernel_cuda(fn, n_warmup=5, n_iter=20):
+    for _ in range(n_warmup):
+        fn()
+    torch.cuda.synchronize()
+    s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
+    e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
+    s.record()
+    for _ in range(n_iter):
+        fn()
+    e.record()
+    torch.cuda.synchronize()
+    return s.elapsed_time(e) / n_iter
+
+
+shapes = [
+    {'T_total': 32768, 'H': 4096, 'I': 1536, 'E': 128, 'K': 8},
+    {'T_total': 4096, 'H': 2048, 'I': 1024, 'E': 64, 'K': 4},
+    {'T_total': 16384, 'H': 2048, 'I': 4096, 'E': 64, 'K': 8},
+]
+
+import reference as ref
+
+# Wider sweep
+configs = [
+    # Best from earlier sweeps
+    (128, 64, 64, 4, 3, 188, 4),
+    # More nw, smaller ns
+    (128, 64, 64, 8, 2, 188, 4),
+    (128, 64, 64, 8, 3, 188, 4),
+    (128, 64, 64, 8, 2, 188, 8),
+    # Smaller M
+    (64, 128, 64, 4, 3, 188, 4),
+    (64, 128, 64, 8, 2, 188, 4),
+    (64, 128, 64, 8, 3, 188, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 4, 4, 188, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 4, 5, 188, 4),
+    (64, 128, 32, 8, 4, 188, 4),
+    # More BN
+    (64, 256, 32, 8, 3, 188, 4),
+    (64, 256, 32, 8, 4, 188, 4),
+    (128, 128, 32, 8, 3, 188, 4),
+    (128, 128, 32, 8, 4, 188, 4),
+    # Even bigger
+    (256, 128, 32, 8, 2, 188, 4),
+    (256, 64, 64, 8, 2, 188, 4),
+    (256, 64, 32, 8, 3, 188, 4),
+]
+
+results = {}
+for shape in shapes:
+    print(f'\n=== Shape: {shape} ===')
+    ref.T_total = shape['T_total']; ref.H = shape['H']; ref.I = shape['I']; ref.E = shape['E']; ref.K = shape['K']
+
+    init_args = ref.get_init_inputs()
+    ref_model = ref.Model(*init_args).cuda().eval()
+    W_gate = ref_model.W_gate
+    W_up = ref_model.W_up
+    hidden = torch.randn(shape['T_total']*shape['K'], shape['H'], dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda') * 0.1
+    T_perm = shape['T_total'] * shape['K']
+    base = T_perm // shape['E']
+    rem = T_perm - base * shape['E']
+    counts = torch.full((shape['E'],), base, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
+    counts[:rem] += 1
+    offsets = torch.zeros(shape['E']+1, dtype=torch.int32, device='cuda')
+    offsets[1:] = torch.cumsum(counts, dim=0)
+
+    for cfg in configs:
+        BM, BN, BK, nw, ns, ns_sms, gm = cfg
+        try:
+            bte, btma = _build_block_table(offsets, shape['E'], BM)
+            nmb = bte.shape[0]
+            nnb = (shape['I'] + BN - 1) // BN
+            nt = nmb * nnb
+            out = torch.empty(T_perm, shape['I'], dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+
+            def fn(h=hidden, o=offsets, wg=W_gate, wu=W_up, BM=BM, BN=BN, BK=BK, nw=nw, ns=ns, ns_sms=ns_sms, gm=gm, bte=bte, btma=btma, nmb=nmb, nnb=nnb, nt=nt, out=out):
+                _kernel[(ns_sms,)](
+                    h, wg, wu, out,
+                    bte, btma,
+                    shape['H'], shape['I'],
+                    nmb, nnb, nt,
+                    h.stride(0), h.stride(1),
+                    wg.stride(0), wg.stride(1), wg.stride(2),
+

 # (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N, BLOCK_K, num_warps, num_stages, GROUP_M)
 def _pick_config(T_total: int, H: int, I: int, E: int, K: int):
+    """Per-shape config picker based on benchmark sweep.
+
+    T_perm is the actual token count routed.
+    """
+    T_perm = T_total * K
+    avg_tokens = T_perm // E
+    # Shape 0 (H=4096, I=1536): BM=256 nw=8 wins (40.8 TFLOPs vs 40.0)
+    if T_total == 32768 and H == 4096:
+        return (256, 64, 32, 8, 3, 4)
+    # Shape 2 (H=2048, I=4096): BM=256 nw=8 wins (40.8 vs 39.8)
+    if T_total == 16384 and H == 2048 and I == 4096:
+        return (256, 64, 64, 8, 2, 4)
+    # Shape 1 (small, H=2048, I=1024): BM=128 nw=4 wins (77.9 TFLOPs)
     return (128, 64, 64, 4, 3, 4)
